## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Envoy HTTP/1.1 to HTTP/2 Header Normalization Migration

## Your Task

Find all C++ source files in envoyproxy/envoy that handle HTTP/1.1 to HTTP/2 header translation: the header case normalization (lowercase), the pseudo-header injection (:method, :path, :scheme, :authority), and the upgrade header handling.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2, sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367, sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6, sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e.

I am thinking...: Now I have a clear picture of the HTTP/1.1 to HTTP/2 header translation in `source/common/http/http1/codec_impl.cc`:

1. **Header case normalization (lowercase)**: Line 565 - `current_header_field_.inlineTransform([](char c) { return absl::ascii_tolower(c); });` in `completeCurrentHeader()`

2. **Pseudo-header injection**:
   - `:method` - Line 1218: `headers->setMethod(parser_->methodName());` in `onHeadersCompleteBase()`
   - `:path` - Line 1111/1125/1159: `headers.addViaMove(std::move(path), ...)` and `headers.setPath(...)` in `handlePath()`

3. **Upgrade header handling**: Lines 849-870 in `onHeadersCompleteImpl()` - handling upgrade headers including h2c upgrade removal

392026-03-08T21:22:16.112855agentmessage-
I am thinking...: Now I have a comprehensive picture. Let me summarize the key files and functions:

## Files involved in HTTP/1.1 to HTTP/2 header translation:

### 1. `source/common/http/http1/codec_impl.cc` - PRIMARY FILE
This is the main file for HTTP/1.1 codec implementation. Key functions:
- **`completeCurrentHeader()`** (line 542): Performs **lowercase normalization** of header names using `current_header_field_.inlineTransform([](char c) { return absl::ascii_tolower(c); });`
- **`handlePath()`** (line 1100): Injects **`:path`** and **`:scheme`** pseudo-headers from the HTTP/1.1 request URL
- **`onHeadersCompleteBase()`** (line 1186): Injects **`:method`** pseudo-header via `headers->setMethod(parser_->methodName())`; also handles upgrade headers
- **`onHeadersCompleteImpl()`** (line 836): Handles upgrade header processing (h2c upgrade removal, CONNECT handling)
- **`encodeHeadersBase()`** (line 138): Translates **`:authority`** → `host` when encoding HTTP/1.1 responses (reverse direction)
- **`RequestEncoderImpl::encodeHeaders()`** (line 440): Encodes HTTP/2 internal representation back to HTTP/1.1 wire format

### 2. `source/common/http/http1/header_formatter.cc`
- **`ProperCaseHeaderKeyFormatter::format()`**: Handles proper case formatting of header keys (optional, for HTTP/1.1 output)

### 3. `source/common/http/conn_manager_utility.cc` - IMPORTANT
- **`mutateRequestHeaders()`** (line 79): Handles upgrade header removal (Connection, Upgrade headers), TE header sanitization, and **`:scheme`** injection
- **`sanitizeTEHeader()`** (line 292): Sanitizes TE header for HTTP/2 compatibility

### 4. `source/common/http/utility.cc` - UPGRADE HANDLING
- **`transformUpgradeRequestFromH1toH2()`** (line 1047): Transforms HTTP/1.1 Upgrade requests to HTTP/2 CONNECT+:protoc
... (truncated)

## Key Files for HTTP/1.1 to HTTP/2 Header Translation in Envoy

### 1. Header Case Normalization (Lowercase)
**`source/common/http/http1/codec_impl.cc`** — `completeCurrentHeader()` (line 565):
```cpp
current_header_field_.inlineTransform([](char c) { return absl::ascii_tolower(c); });
```
This is the primary site where HTTP/1.1 header names are lowercased to comply with HTTP/2's requirement.

### 2. Pseudo-Header Injection
**`source/common/http/http1/codec_impl.cc`**:
- **`handlePath()`** — Injects `:path`, `:scheme`, and `:authority` (host) from the HTTP/1.1 request URL
- **`onHeadersCompleteBase()`** — Injects `:method` via `headers->setMethod(parser_->methodName())`

**`source/common/http/conn_manager_utility.cc`** — `mutateRequestHeaders()`:
- Injects/normalizes `:scheme` based on X-Forwarded-Proto or TLS status

### 3. Upgrade Header Handling
**`source/common/http/utility.cc`**:
- `transformUpgradeRequestFromH1toH2()` — Converts HTTP/1.1 Upgrade to HTTP/2 extended CONNECT (sets `:method=CONNECT`, `:protocol=<upgrade-value>`, removes `Upgrade`/`Connection`)
- `transformUpgradeResponseFromH1toH2()` — Converts HTTP/1.1 101 to HTTP/2 200

**`source/common/http/http1/codec_impl.cc`** — `onHeadersCompleteImpl()`:
- Removes unsupported h2c upgrade headers
- Sets `handling_upgrade_` flag for valid upgrades

**`source/common/http/http2/codec_impl.cc`** — `ClientStreamImpl::encodeHeaders()`:
- Calls `transformUpgradeRequestFromH1toH2()` when encoding upgrade requests to HTTP/2 upstream
